function getBoundsZoomLevel(bd, mapDim) {
 var WORLD_DIM = { height: 256, width: 256 };
 var ZOOM_MAX = 21;
 function latRad(lat) { var sin = Math.sin(lat * Math.PI / 180); var radX2 = Math.log((1 + sin) / (1 - sin)) / 2; return Math.max(Math.min(radX2, Math.PI), -Math.PI) / 2;}
 function zoom(mapPx, worldPx, fraction) {return Math.floor(Math.log(mapPx / worldPx / fraction) / Math.LN2);}
 var ne = bd.getNorthEast();
 var sw = bd.getSouthWest();
 var latFraction = (latRad(ne.lat()) - latRad(sw.lat())) / Math.PI;
 var lngDiff = ne.lng() - sw.lng();
 var lngFraction = ((lngDiff < 0) ? (lngDiff + 360) : lngDiff) / 360;
 var latZoom = zoom(mapDim.height, WORLD_DIM.height, latFraction);
 var lngZoom = zoom(mapDim.width, WORLD_DIM.width, lngFraction);
 return Math.min(latZoom, lngZoom, ZOOM_MAX);
}

 var map_google = new google.maps.Map(gc,mapOptions);
}

function pad(s)
{
return ((s.toString().length==1) ? "0"+s : s);
}

function showtm(df)
{
sda.setSeconds(sda.getSeconds()+df);
hr=sda.getHours();
adm="AM";
if (hr>11) adm="PM";
if (hr>12) hr-=12; 
if (hr==0) hr=12;
document.getElementById("ourtime").innerHTML=hr+":"+pad(sda.getMinutes())+":"+pad(sda.getSeconds())+" "+adm;
}

var isIE    = (/msie/i.test(navigator.userAgent) && !/opera/i.test(navigator.userAgent));    
var colurl = '/cost-of-living/col.php';
  
var coldefaultstate = 'CA';
var coldefaultcity = 'Julian';

function colAjaxRequest(reset) {
    var req = false;
    // Opera, Mozilla, etc.
    if(window.XMLHttpRequest){req=new XMLHttpRequest();if(!isIE && req.overrideMimetype){req.overrideMimeType('text/plain');}} 
    //IE
    else if(window.ActiveXObject){try{req=new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");}catch(e){try{req=new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");} catch(e){}}}    
    
    req.onreadystatechange = function() { if (req.readyState == 4 && ((req.status == 0) || (req.status == 200))) { colHandleRequest(req); } };
    if(reset==true)
    {
        req.open('GET', '/cost-of-living/col.php');
        req.send(null);            
    } else if(colCreateUrl()==true) {
        req.open('GET', colurl);
        req.send(null);    
    } 
}

function colHandleRequest(req) {    
    var ac = document.getElementById('colForm');
    ac.innerHTML = req.responseText;
    
    var originstate = document.getElementById('originstate');
    if(originstate && originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value == '')
    {
        originstate.value = coldefaultstate;
    }    
    var origincity = document.getElementById('origincity');
    if(origincity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value == '')
    {
        var coli,coll=origincity.length;
        for(coli=0;coli<coll;coli++){
            if(origincity[coli].text==coldefaultcity)
            {
                origincity.value = origincity[coli].value;
            }    
        }
    }        
}

function colCreateUrl() {
    colurl = '/cost-of-living/col.php';    
    var salary = document.getElementById('salary');
    if(salary)
    {
        colurl = colurl + '?salary=' + salary.value;
        
        var originstate = document.getElementById('originstate');
        var destinationstate = document.getElementById('destinationstate');
        var origincity = document.getElementById('origincity');
        var destinationcity = document.getElementById('destinationcity');
        
        if(originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&originstate=' + originstate.value; }
        if(destinationstate.value != 'undefined' && destinationstate.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&destinationstate=' + destinationstate.value; }

        if(origincity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&origincity=' + origincity.value; }
        if(destinationcity && destinationcity.value != 'undefined' && destinationcity.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&destinationcity=' + destinationcity.value; }

        if(origincity && destinationcity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value != '' && destinationcity.value != 'undefined' && destinationcity.value != '')        
        {
            return true;
        }   

        if(!origincity && !destinationcity && originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value != '' && destinationstate.value != 'undefined' && destinationstate.value != '')        
        {
            return true;
        }    
        
        return false;
    }    
}

    element = $('body');
    offset = element.offset();

function T$(i) { return document.getElementById(i) }
function T$$(e, p) { return p.getElementsByTagName(e) }

TINY.table = function() {
    function sorter(n) { this.n = n; this.sortD = 0; this.sortC = 0}
    
	sorter.prototype.init = function(e, f, r) {
        var t = ge(e), i = 0; this.e = e; this.l = t.r.length; t.a = [];
        t.h = T$$('thead', T$(e))[0].rows[r]; t.w = t.h.cells.length;
        for (i; i < t.w; i++) {
            var c = t.h.cells[i];
            if (c.className != 'nosort') {
            
				var icon = "<span class='badge alert-info'>" + 
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort-by-attributes-alt' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort-by-attributes' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "</span>";
            
				$(c).prepend(icon);
                c.className = this.head;
                c.onclick = new Function('window.sortableTables["' + this.n + '"].wk(this.cellIndex)')
            }
        }
        for (i = 0; i < this.l; i++) { t.a[i] = {} }		
        if (f != -1) t.h.cells[f].className = (this.sortD) ? this.desc : this.asc;
    };
    sorter.prototype.wk = function(y) {
        var t = ge(this.e), x = t.h.cells[y], i = 0;
        for (i; i < this.l; i++) {
            t.a[i].o = i; var v = t.r[i].cells[y];
			t.a[i].v = v.textContent || v.innerText;
        }

        if ((x.className == this.head)) { t.d = 0; t.p = y; x.className = this.asc; t.a.sort(cp); }
		$("#" + this.e + " th").removeClass().addClass(this.head);
        if (t.p == y) { t.a.reverse(); x.className = t.d ? this.asc : this.desc; t.d = t.d ? 0 : 1 }
        else { t.p = y; t.a.sort(cp); t.d = 0; x.className = this.asc }

        var n = document.createElement('tbody');
        for (i = 0; i < this.l; i++) {
            var r = t.r[t.a[i].o].cloneNode(true);
            r.className = t.r[t.a[i].o].className;
            n.appendChild(r);
        }
        t.replaceChild(n, t.b);

        this.sortC = y;
        this.sortD = t.d;
    };

    function ge(e) { var t = T$(e); t.b = T$$('tbody', t)[0]; t.r = t.b.rows; return t };
    function cp(f, c) {
        var g, h; f = g = f.v.toLowerCase(), c = h = c.v.toLowerCase();
        var i = parseFloat(f.replace(/(\$|\,|\%|over| \>|\+)/g, '')), n = parseFloat(c.replace(/(\$|\,|\%|over |\>|\+)/g, ''));
        if (!isNaN(i) && !isNaN(n)) { g = i, h = n }
        return g > h ? 1 : (g < h ? -1 : 0)
    };
    return { sorter: sorter }
} ();

$(function(){
    function run(){
            function formatItemAutocomplete(row) {
                if(typeof(row[1]) != "undefined" && row[1] !== null) {
                    return row[0] + " (<i>pop. " + row[1] + "</i>)";
                }
            }

            $("#city_left").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })


            $("#city_right").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })
            $(".btn-submit").click(function () {
                $("#city_form").submit();
            });

            $('#city_left').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });
            $('#city_right').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });

    }
    run();
});

 (function($) {
 
 function has3d() {
 
 if (window.ua.mobile) return false;
 if (!window.getComputedStyle) return false;
 

 var el = document.createElement('p'), 
 has3d,
 transforms = {
 'webkitTransform':'-webkit-transform',
 'OTransform':'-o-transform',
 'msTransform':'-ms-transform',
 'MozTransform':'-moz-transform',
 'transform':'transform'
 };
 
 // Add it to the body to get the computed style.
 document.body.insertBefore(el, null);

 for (var t in transforms) {
 if (el.style[t] !== undefined) {
 el.style[t] = "translate3d(1px,1px,1px)";
 has3d = window.getComputedStyle(el).getPropertyValue(transforms[t]);
 }
 }

 document.body.removeChild(el);

 return (has3d !== undefined && has3d.length > 0 && has3d !== "none");
 }


 function flipItInit()
 {
 $('body').off('mousemove',flipItInit);
 
 if (!has3d()) return;
 
 // if it's supported, remove the scroll effect add the cool card flipping instead
 $('.thumb.scroll').removeClass('scroll').addClass('flip');	
 //secure IE11 from flipping image during page load
 $('.thumb-detail').css("display","block");
 
 // add/remove flip class that make the transition effect
 $('.thumb.flip').hover(
 function () {$(this).find('.thumb-wrapper').addClass('flipIt');},
 function () {$(this).find('.thumb-wrapper').removeClass('flipIt');}
 );
 };
 
 $('body').on('mousemove',flipItInit);
 
 })(jQuery); /* city/local-time.js */

$(window).on('load', function(){
	var minYear = 2000;
	var maxYear = 2013;
	var months = [];
	var tickPositions = [];
	for (var year = minYear; year <= maxYear; year++)
	{
	for (var month = 0; month < 12; month++)
	months.push(Date.UTC(year, month, 1));
	tickPositions.push(Date.UTC(year, 5, 1));
	}
	$("#air-pollution-chart .chart").each(function(chart_idx, chart) {
	var $chart = $(chart);
	var options = $chart.data('chart');
	var newSeries = $.map(options.series, function(series) {
	var newData = $.map(series.data, function(value, idx) { return {x: months[idx], y: value}; });
	return $.extend({}, series, {data: newData});
	});
	options = $.extend({}, options, {series: newSeries});
	$.when(city_graphing.ready).then(function(){
	$chart.highcharts(options);
	});

	});
});

function getBoundsZoomLevel(bd, mapDim) {
 var WORLD_DIM = { height: 256, width: 256 };
 var ZOOM_MAX = 21;
 function latRad(lat) { var sin = Math.sin(lat * Math.PI / 180); var radX2 = Math.log((1 + sin) / (1 - sin)) / 2; return Math.max(Math.min(radX2, Math.PI), -Math.PI) / 2;}
 function zoom(mapPx, worldPx, fraction) {return Math.floor(Math.log(mapPx / worldPx / fraction) / Math.LN2);}
 var ne = bd.getNorthEast();
 var sw = bd.getSouthWest();
 var latFraction = (latRad(ne.lat()) - latRad(sw.lat())) / Math.PI;
 var lngDiff = ne.lng() - sw.lng();
 var lngFraction = ((lngDiff < 0) ? (lngDiff + 360) : lngDiff) / 360;
 var latZoom = zoom(mapDim.height, WORLD_DIM.height, latFraction);
 var lngZoom = zoom(mapDim.width, WORLD_DIM.width, lngFraction);
 return Math.min(latZoom, lngZoom, ZOOM_MAX);
}

 var zlev = getBoundsZoomLevel(new google.maps.LatLngBounds(new google.maps.LatLng(33.0320,-116.6246),new google.maps.LatLng(33.1099,-116.5466)), {width:parseInt(gc.style.width), height:parseInt(gc.style.height)});

 var map_google = new google.maps.Map(gc,mapOptions);
}

function pad(s)
{
return ((s.toString().length==1) ? "0"+s : s);
}

function showtm(df)
{
sda.setSeconds(sda.getSeconds()+df);

adm="AM";
if (hr>11) adm="PM";

}

var isIE    = (/msie/i.test(navigator.userAgent) && !/opera/i.test(navigator.userAgent));    
var colurl = '/cost-of-living/col.php';
  
var coldefaultstate = 'CA';
var coldefaultcity = 'Julian';

function colAjaxRequest(reset) {
    var req = false;
    // Opera, Mozilla, etc.
    if(window.XMLHttpRequest){req=new XMLHttpRequest();if(!isIE && req.overrideMimetype){req.overrideMimeType('text/plain');}} 
    //IE
    else if(window.ActiveXObject){try{req=new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");}catch(e){try{req=new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");} catch(e){}}}    
    
    req.onreadystatechange = function() { if (req.readyState == 4 && ((req.status == 0) || (req.status == 200))) { colHandleRequest(req); } };
    if(reset==true)
    {
        req.open('GET', '/cost-of-living/col.php');
        req.send(null);            
    } else if(colCreateUrl()==true) {
        req.open('GET', colurl);
        req.send(null);    
    } 
}

function colHandleRequest(req) {    
    var ac = document.getElementById('colForm');
    ac.innerHTML = req.responseText;
    
    var originstate = document.getElementById('originstate');
    if(originstate && originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value == '')
    {
        originstate.value = coldefaultstate;
    }    
    var origincity = document.getElementById('origincity');
    if(origincity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value == '')
    {
        var coli,coll=origincity.length;
        for(coli=0;coli<coll;coli++){
            if(origincity[coli].text==coldefaultcity)
            {
                origincity.value = origincity[coli].value;
            }    
        }
    }        
}

function colCreateUrl() {
    colurl = '/cost-of-living/col.php';    
    var salary = document.getElementById('salary');
    if(salary)
    {
        colurl = colurl + '?salary=' + salary.value;
        
        var originstate = document.getElementById('originstate');
        var destinationstate = document.getElementById('destinationstate');
        var origincity = document.getElementById('origincity');
        var destinationcity = document.getElementById('destinationcity');
        
        if(originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&originstate=' + originstate.value; }
        if(destinationstate.value != 'undefined' && destinationstate.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&destinationstate=' + destinationstate.value; }

        if(origincity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&origincity=' + origincity.value; }
        if(destinationcity && destinationcity.value != 'undefined' && destinationcity.value != '') { colurl = colurl + '&destinationcity=' + destinationcity.value; }

        if(origincity && destinationcity && origincity.value != 'undefined' && origincity.value != '' && destinationcity.value != 'undefined' && destinationcity.value != '')        
        {
            return true;
        }   

        if(!origincity && !destinationcity && originstate.value != 'undefined' && originstate.value != '' && destinationstate.value != 'undefined' && destinationstate.value != '')        
        {
            return true;
        }    
        
        return false;
    }    
}

    verticalOffset = typeof(verticalOffset) != 'undefined' ? verticalOffset : 0;
    element = $('body');
    offset = element.offset();
    offsetTop = offset.top;
    $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: offsetTop}, 500, 'linear');

var TINY = {};
function T$(i) { return document.getElementById(i) }
function T$$(e, p) { return p.getElementsByTagName(e) }

TINY.table = function() {
    function sorter(n) { this.n = n; this.sortD = 0; this.sortC = 0}
    
	sorter.prototype.init = function(e, f, r) {
        var t = ge(e), i = 0; this.e = e; this.l = t.r.length; t.a = [];
        t.h = T$$('thead', T$(e))[0].rows[r]; t.w = t.h.cells.length;
        for (i; i < t.w; i++) {
            var c = t.h.cells[i];
            if (c.className != 'nosort') {
            
				var icon = "<span class='badge alert-info'>" + 
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort-by-attributes-alt' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort-by-attributes' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "<span class='glyphicon glyphicon-sort' aria-hidden='true'></span>" +
				           "</span>";
            
				$(c).prepend(icon);
                c.className = this.head;
                c.onclick = new Function('window.sortableTables["' + this.n + '"].wk(this.cellIndex)')
            }
        }
        for (i = 0; i < this.l; i++) { t.a[i] = {} }		
        if (f != -1) t.h.cells[f].className = (this.sortD) ? this.desc : this.asc;
    };
    sorter.prototype.wk = function(y) {
        var t = ge(this.e), x = t.h.cells[y], i = 0;
        for (i; i < this.l; i++) {
            t.a[i].o = i; var v = t.r[i].cells[y];
			t.a[i].v = v.textContent || v.innerText;
        }

        if ((x.className == this.head)) { t.d = 0; t.p = y; x.className = this.asc; t.a.sort(cp); }
		$("#" + this.e + " th").removeClass().addClass(this.head);
        if (t.p == y) { t.a.reverse(); x.className = t.d ? this.asc : this.desc; t.d = t.d ? 0 : 1 }
        else { t.p = y; t.a.sort(cp); t.d = 0; x.className = this.asc }

        var n = document.createElement('tbody');
        for (i = 0; i < this.l; i++) {
            var r = t.r[t.a[i].o].cloneNode(true);
            r.className = t.r[t.a[i].o].className;
            n.appendChild(r);
        }
        t.replaceChild(n, t.b);

        this.sortC = y;
        this.sortD = t.d;
    };

    function ge(e) { var t = T$(e); t.b = T$$('tbody', t)[0]; t.r = t.b.rows; return t };
    function cp(f, c) {
        var g, h; f = g = f.v.toLowerCase(), c = h = c.v.toLowerCase();
        var i = parseFloat(f.replace(/(\$|\,|\%|over| \>|\+)/g, '')), n = parseFloat(c.replace(/(\$|\,|\%|over |\>|\+)/g, ''));
        if (!isNaN(i) && !isNaN(n)) { g = i, h = n }
        return g > h ? 1 : (g < h ? -1 : 0)
    };
    return { sorter: sorter }
} ();

$(function(){
    function run(){
            function formatItemAutocomplete(row) {
                if(typeof(row[1]) != "undefined" && row[1] !== null) {
                    return row[0] + " (<i>pop. " + row[1] + "</i>)";
                }
            }

            $("#city_left").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })


            $("#city_right").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })
            $(".btn-submit").click(function () {
                $("#city_form").submit();
            });

            $('#city_left').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });
            $('#city_right').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });

    }
    run();
});

 (function($) {
 
 function has3d() {
 
 if (window.ua.mobile) return false;
 if (!window.getComputedStyle) return false;
 

 var el = document.createElement('p'), 
 has3d,
 transforms = {
 'webkitTransform':'-webkit-transform',
 'OTransform':'-o-transform',
 'msTransform':'-ms-transform',
 'MozTransform':'-moz-transform',
 'transform':'transform'
 };
 
 // Add it to the body to get the computed style.
 document.body.insertBefore(el, null);

 for (var t in transforms) {
 if (el.style[t] !== undefined) {
 el.style[t] = "translate3d(1px,1px,1px)";
 has3d = window.getComputedStyle(el).getPropertyValue(transforms[t]);
 }
 }

 document.body.removeChild(el);

 return (has3d !== undefined && has3d.length > 0 && has3d !== "none");
 }


 function flipItInit()
 {
 $('body').off('mousemove',flipItInit);
 
 if (!has3d()) return;
 
 // if it's supported, remove the scroll effect add the cool card flipping instead
 $('.thumb.scroll').removeClass('scroll').addClass('flip');	
 //secure IE11 from flipping image during page load
 $('.thumb-detail').css("display","block");
 
 // add/remove flip class that make the transition effect
 $('.thumb.flip').hover(
 function () {$(this).find('.thumb-wrapper').addClass('flipIt');},
 function () {$(this).find('.thumb-wrapper').removeClass('flipIt');}
 );
 };
 
 $('body').on('mousemove',flipItInit);
 
 })(jQuery); /* city/local-time.js */

$(window).on('load', function(){
	var minYear = 2000;
	var maxYear = 2013;
	var months = [];
	var tickPositions = [];
	for (var year = minYear; year <= maxYear; year++)
	{
	for (var month = 0; month < 12; month++)
	months.push(Date.UTC(year, month, 1));
	tickPositions.push(Date.UTC(year, 5, 1));
	}
	$("#air-pollution-chart .chart").each(function(chart_idx, chart) {
	var $chart = $(chart);
	var options = $chart.data('chart');
	var newSeries = $.map(options.series, function(series) {
	var newData = $.map(series.data, function(value, idx) { return {x: months[idx], y: value}; });
	return $.extend({}, series, {data: newData});
	});
	options = $.extend({}, options, {series: newSeries});
	$.when(city_graphing.ready).then(function(){
	$chart.highcharts(options);
	});

	});
});
